### [1] [Non-perturbative determination of the QCD Equation of State up to the electroweak scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09330)
*Michele Pepe*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文非微扰地确定了具有三个无质量夸克味的QCD状态方程，覆盖从电弱能标到3 GeV的宽温区，并与低温区平滑连接；发现即使在接近电弱能标的高温下，仍需引入超越已知微扰级数的非微扰贡献才能准确描述状态方程；所用方法结合了位移边界条件和基于非微扰定义的重整化耦合跑动来确定恒定物理线，该方法具有一般性，可推广至含四或五种有质量夸克味的QCD。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索QCD在高温（尤其是电弱能标附近）下的非微扰行为，弥补此前高温度区域缺乏非微扰研究的空白，并检验微扰理论的有效范围。

Method: 采用位移边界条件（shifted boundary conditions）结合基于非微扰定义的重整化耦合跑动来确定恒定物理线（lines of constant physics），从而实现对高温区QCD状态方程的非微扰格点计算。

Result: 成功获得N_f=3质量为零夸克情形下跨越电弱能标至3 GeV的非微扰QCD状态方程；发现标准微扰展开不足以描述该温区热力学量，必须包含高阶乃至非微扰修正项。

Conclusion: QCD在高温（直至电弱能标）仍受显著非微扰效应影响；所发展的方法为未来研究更现实的多味（如N_f=4,5）QCD热力学提供了通用框架。

Abstract: The QCD Equation of State with $N_f=3$ massless quark flavours is determined non-perturbatively over a broad range of temperatures, extending from the electroweak scale down to 3 GeV, and smoothly connecting to the low-temperature regime. The comparison with perturbative predictions shows that, even at temperatures approaching the electroweak scale, the Equation of State can be accurately described only by adding terms beyond the known perturbative series, including non-perturbative contributions. The strategy that allows this investigation in the previously unexplored high-temperature regime combines shifted boundary conditions with a determination of the lines of constant physics based on the running of a non-perturbatively defined renormalized coupling. This methodology is general and can be applied to QCD with four or five massive quark flavours.

</details>


### [2] [How to formulate the $\mathbb{Z}_8$ topological invariant of Majorana fermion on the lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09354)
*Sho Araki,Hidenori Fukaya,Tetsuya Onogi,Satoshi Yamaguchi*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出了Arf-Brown-Kervaire (ABK) 不变量在格点规范理论中的实现方法，通过Wilson Dirac算子的Pfaffian提取Z8值ABK不变量，并在二维格点上进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展格点规范理论中拓扑不变量的定义，特别是对非定向流形上具有反射对称性的Majorana费米子系统中的ABK不变量进行格点实现。

Method: 利用Wilson Dirac算子的Pfaffian，在考虑边界条件（含/不含domain-wall质量项）下提取ABK不变量，并在二维格点（环面、克莱因瓶、实射影平面、莫比乌斯带）上进行数值验证。

Result: 成功实现了ABK不变量的格点构造，数值结果与连续理论中Z8值一致。

Conclusion: ABK不变量可在格点上通过Wilson Dirac算子的Pfaffian可靠提取，为研究非定向流形上的拓扑反常和对称保护相提供了新工具。

Abstract: Topological invariants and their associated anomalies have played a crucial role in understanding low-energy phenomena in quantum field theories. In lattice gauge theory, the standard $\mathbb{Z}$-valued Atiyah-Singer index is formulated via the overlap Dirac operator through the Ginsparg-Wilson relation, but extensions to more general topological invariants have remained limited. In this work, we propose a lattice formulation of the Arf-Brown-Kervaire (ABK) invariant, which takes values in $\mathbb{Z}_8$. The ABK invariant arises in Majorana fermion partition functions with reflection symmetry on two-dimensional non-oriented manifolds, and its definition involves an infinite sum over Dirac eigenvalues that must be properly regularized. By carefully treating the boundary conditions, with and without a domain-wall mass term, we demonstrate that the ABK invariant can be extracted from Pfaffians of the Wilson Dirac operator. We further provide numerical verification on two-dimensional lattices, showing that the $\mathbb{Z}_8$-valued results on the torus, Klein bottle, real projective plane, and Möbius strip agree with those in the continuum theory.

</details>


### [3] [First-Principles Determination of the Proton-Proton Fusion Matrix Element from Lattice QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09554)
*Zi-Yu Wang,Xu Feng,Bo-Hao Jian,Lu-Chang Jin,Chuan Liu*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过格点QCD计算了质子-质子融合反应的矩阵元，首次在非物理夸克质量下实现了包含有限体积修正和两核子散射效应的完整分析，揭示了二体力贡献及当前精度限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质子-质子融合是恒星能量产生的起始弱相互作用，其第一性原理计算是核理论长期目标；现有格点QCD计算尚缺乏对有限体积效应和两核子再散射的系统处理。

Method: 采用m_π≈432 MeV的格点QCD模拟，结合Lellouch-Lüscher有限体积修正（2+J→2框架），引入双局域核子插值算符与变分分析压制激发态污染，并利用Lüscher公式提取两核子能谱与散射参数。

Result: 得到未含再散射修正的归一化矩阵元<d|J|pp>/g_A = 0.984(10)，表明存在小但非零的二体力流贡献；计入再散射后，LL因子显著改变二体力贡献，而两核子散射参数的大误差强烈影响有限体积修正；最终给出低能常数L_{1,A}=6.0(7.1) fm³，与唯象值在自然性尺度上一致。

Conclusion: 该工作验证了基于格点QCD从头计算弱两核反应的可行性，同时揭示了当前在物理π质量下实现高精度计算所面临的核心挑战，为后续研究奠定基础。

Abstract: Proton-proton fusion is the fundamental weak reaction initiating stellar energy production, and a first-principles determination of its matrix element remains a long-standing goal of nuclear theory. We present a lattice QCD calculation of the pp fusion matrix element at m_pi~432 MeV. We implement Lellouch-Luscher (LL) finite-volume (FV) corrections within a 2+J->2 framework, accounting for two-nucleon (2N) rescattering, to relate FV matrix elements to infinite-volume counterparts. Excited-state contamination is suppressed using bi-local nucleon-nucleon interpolating operators and a variational analysis with three lowest momenta. This enables determination of 2N energy spectrum and scattering parameters via Luscher's FV formalism. Before including rescattering effects in the LL factor, we obtain <d|J|pp>/g_A = 0.984(10), where g_A is the axial charge. The deviation from unity indicates a small nonvanishing 2-body current contribution. Our analysis shows that rescattering effects in LL factors substantially modify the 2-body contribution, while large uncertainties in 2N scattering parameters propagate strongly into FV corrections. Thus, precise determination of the 2-body low-energy constant L_{1,A} remains highly challenging with current lattice inputs. Despite the large uncertainty, L_{1,A}=6.0(7.1) fm^3 is compatible, at the level of naturalness, with phenomenological extractions. This work demonstrates feasibility and intrinsic challenges of ab initio lattice QCD calculations of weak 2N reactions, and establishes a foundation for future studies at or near the physical pion mass.

</details>


### [4] [Phase diagram of 4D SU(3) Yang-Mills theory at $θ=π$ via imaginary theta simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09604)
*Akira Matsumoto,Mitsuaki Hirasawa,Jun Nishimura,Atis Yosprakob*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文通过虚θ参数模拟和解析延拓方法，研究了4D SU(3)杨-米尔斯理论在θ=π时CP对称性的自发破缺与恢复问题，并利用stout抹平技术与重加权方法获得初步结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接模拟θ=π时存在严重符号问题，难以研究CP对称性是否在禁闭相自发破缺及是否在退禁闭温度精确恢复。

Method: 采用虚θ参数模拟，结合解析延拓至实θ；在混合蒙特卡洛模拟中引入stout抹平技术以恢复规范场拓扑性质；利用关于抹平步长参数的重加权方法研究观测量对抹平时间的依赖性，并识别标度区域；在该区域计算CP对称性序参量。

Result: 观测到观测量随抹平时间呈现清晰标度行为；在标度区域内计算得到CP对称性破缺的初步证据及对称性恢复温度的初步结果。

Conclusion: 支持CP对称性在禁闭相自发破缺、并在退禁闭温度附近恢复的猜想，但需进一步系统误差分析确认。

Abstract: It has been speculated that the CP symmetry of 4D SU(3) Yang-Mills theory at $θ=π$ is spontaneously broken in the confined phase, and it is recovered precisely at the deconfining temperature. The direct simulation of the theory at $θ=π$ is, however, difficult due to the sign problem. We therefore simulate the theory with an imaginary theta parameter and perform analytic continuation to the real theta to explore the phase diagram. We implement the stout smearing technique in the hybrid Monte Carlo simulation to recover the topological property of the gauge field. The smearing-time dependence of the observable is investigated using the reweighting method with respect to the smearing step parameters, and a clear scaling behavior is observed. The order parameter of the CP symmetry is then computed in the scaling region to detect symmetry breaking. We report preliminary results on the expected CP breaking and restoration temperature.

</details>

### [5] [Binary Black Holes population synthesis based on the current LVK observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08785)
*Mehdi El Bouhaddouti,Ilias Cholis,Muhsin Aljaf*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）2015–2024年观测数据，检验双黑洞并合事件的种群合成模型，发现观测数据显著支持包含恒星坍缩形成的一代黑洞（幂律质量分布）与分层并合产生的二代黑洞的混合种群，并提示可能还需引入原初黑洞作为第三类成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解双黑洞并合事件的形成机制和环境，检验当前观测是否仅能由恒星演化产生的一代黑洞解释，或需引入分层并合及原初黑洞等额外形成通道。

Method: 基于LVK 2015–2024年观测的双黑洞样本，采用贝叶斯统计方法比较不同种群模型（纯幂律、幂律+分层并合、三成分混合）的似然与贝叶斯因子。

Result: 数据强烈支持混合种群模型（幂律+分层并合），log-Bayes因子达71；两类黑洞比例可达1:1；加入原初黑洞作为第三成分进一步提升拟合优度。

Conclusion: LVK观测揭示双黑洞种群具有多源性，除恒星起源外，分层并合乃至原初黑洞均可能贡献可观测信号，挑战单一形成模型。

Abstract: The ongoing observations from ground based gravitational-wave observatories have led to the detection of more than a hundred merger events between black holes. We use the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) observations from 2015 to early 2024, to test the population synthesis of these merging binaries; which will allow us to probe the formation mechanisms and environments of these black holes. We test if the current sample of binary black holes can be explained only by the merger of black holes coming from the collapse of the cores of massive stars, i.e. as just first generation black holes merging with each other. Those black holes' masses will roughly follow a power-law distribution. We also test if in addition to the merger between first generation black holes, there is evidence for a second population of black hole binaries in which at least one the binaries' members is the product of an earlier merger between black holes. These binaries are typically referred to as signals of hierarchical mergers. Such a population can possibly explain the observation of very massive black hole binaries by the LVK collaboration. We find that the LVK observations give a statistical preference in log-likelihood of up to $- 2 Δln\mathcal{L} = -150$ or in log-Bayes factor of up to $ln\textrm{BF} = 71$, for the full sample of black hole binaries originating from a combination of black holes following a power-law distribution and black holes from hierarchical mergers. The ratio of black holes following a power-law mass-distribution to a mass-distribution expected from hierarchical mergers is found to be as high as one-to-one. We also consider that some of the LVK black hole merging binaries are the result of primordial black holes (PBHs), merging inside dark matter halos and in the intergalactic medium. Adding a third population is preferred. [abridged]

</details>


### [6] [Detecting Axion-like particles using Cosmic Variance Cancellation with CMB and Radio surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08808)
*Harsh Mehta,Anaya Dixit,Suvodip Mukherjee,Joseph Silk*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用宇宙方差抵消（CVC）技术，结合Simons Observatory（SO）和平方公里阵列（SKA）在微波与射电波段的多频观测，探测轴子类粒子（ALPs）的新方法。该方法通过分析CMB光子在星系团磁场中共振转化为ALPs产生的频谱畸变信号，显著提升对ALP-光子耦合强度g_{aγ}及低质量ALP（如m_a=10^{-14} eV）的约束精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子及类轴子粒子（ALPs）是标准模型扩展中自然出现的暗物质候选者；CMB光子在星系团磁场中可共振转换为ALPs，其信号具有特征频谱行为，但传统单频段观测受限于宇宙方差。

Method: 利用SO和SKA在多个微波与射电频段对同一星系团样本进行观测，提取CMB光子-ALP共振转换导致的ALP畸变信号；通过跨频段交叉相关（即宇宙方差抵消，CVC）抑制噪声，提高信噪比；基于不同频带间ALP信号比值的理论频谱依赖性建模并拟合参数。

Result: 相比仅用自相关谱（auto-only spectra），CVC将ALP信号比值参数的测量标准差从5.9×10^{-2}提升至1×10^{-2}（对应m_a=10^{-14} eV）；该方法可普适探测ALP畸变信号，并甄别因频段误判导致的虚假信号。

Conclusion: CVC是一种高效、普适且鲁棒的ALP探测新范式，特别适用于低质量ALP，在SO与SKA时代具备强大发现潜力。

Abstract: Axions and axion-like particles (ALPs) arise naturally in many extensions of the Standard Model and are among the well-motivated candidates for dark matter. In the presence of magnetic fields of galaxy clusters, Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) photons can convert to ALPs, with the efficiency of the process governed by the cluster electron density and magnetic field profiles, the photon--ALP coupling strength ($g_{aγ}$), as well as the frequency ($ν$) of the photon at the redshift of the cluster. The CMB blackbody spectrum suggests that this resonant conversion also takes place at radio wavelengths, following the spectral behaviour of the ALP distortion signal. This opens a new window to search for ALPs using cosmic variance cancellation (CVC), with multi-frequency tracers of the same phenomenon in CMB photon--ALP resonant conversion. The constraints on the ALP signal ratios from different combinations of microwave and radio bands of the Simons Observatory (SO) and the Square Kilometre Array (SKA) can be significantly improved using CVC compared to the case of using auto-only spectra from the two experiments. With the large number of galaxy clusters that will be observed by SO and SKA, we will be able to obtain much more information using CVC, especially for low-mass ALPs with stronger signals. Using the auto-only spectra from galaxy clusters up to redshift $z = 1$ for inference of the normalized ratio parameter, we obtain a standard deviation of $5.9 \times 10^{-2}$ for an ALP mass $m_a = 10^{-14} \, \mathrm{eV}$, which improves to $1 \times 10^{-2}$ using CVC. This method provides a universal probe of the ALP distortion signal using its spectral dependence and can also invalidate false detections of the ALP signal based on its frequency behaviour in different bands.

</details>


### [7] [Statistical consistency of sign-switching vacuum energy with cosmological observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09270)
*Sehjal Khandelwal,Abraão J. S. Capistrano,Suresh Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文评估了ΛCDM及其符号切换扩展Λ_sCDM模型在数据集一致性与晚期预测充分性方面的表现，采用高斯与精确非高斯一致性诊断方法，发现常用高斯张力度量在非高斯后验与强约束数据结合时易夸大不一致性，而精确非高斯参数偏移显示CMB与BAO观测高度一致；Λ_sCDM在中等红移几何兼容性上略有提升，但参数张力减小未必代表预测一致性改善；强调需使用精确、非高斯及预测性诊断以实现稳健的宇宙学模型一致性评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决常用高斯张力度量在处理宽泛非高斯后验与高精度数据结合时可能夸大模型间不一致性的缺陷，提升宇宙学模型一致性评估的可靠性。

Method: 采用高斯与精确非高斯一致性诊断方法，联合分析Planck、ACT、SPT的CMB数据，DESI DR2的BAO数据，以及PantheonPlus+SH0ES的低红移Ia型超新星数据，对ΛCDM和Λ_sCDM模型进行约束与比较。

Result: 精确非高斯参数偏移显示CMB与BAO在两个模型中均高度一致；Λ_sCDM在中等红移几何兼容性上有 modest improvement；但参数张力降低并不等价于预测一致性提升。

Conclusion: 精确、非高斯及预测性诊断对宇宙学模型一致性评估至关重要，单纯依赖高斯近似可能导致误导性结论。

Abstract: We assess dataset agreement and late-time predictive adequacy in $Λ$CDM and its sign-switching extension, $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM, using a suite of Gaussian and exact non-Gaussian consistency diagnostics. Both models are constrained with cosmic microwave background measurements from Planck, ACT, and SPT, baryon acoustic oscillation data from DESI DR2, and low-redshift Type Ia supernova data from PantheonPlus+SH0ES. We find that commonly used Gaussian tension metrics can significantly overstate inconsistencies when broad, non-Gaussian posteriors are combined with tightly constrained datasets. In contrast, the exact non-Gaussian parameter shift indicates excellent consistency between CMB and BAO observations in both models. The $Λ_{\rm s}$CDM extension modestly improves geometric compatibility at intermediate redshifts, although reductions in parameter-level tension do not necessarily imply improved predictive consistency. These results highlight the importance of exact, non-Gaussian, and predictive diagnostics for robust assessments of cosmological model consistency.

</details>


### [8] [Constraints on Neutrino Mass with Void Weak Lensing Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09278)
*Wenshuo Xu,Cheng Zhao,Chen Su,Huanyuan Shan,Yu Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙空洞与弱引力透镜剪切信号的交叉相关（即空洞透镜效应）对总中微子质量的限制能力，发现其可独立约束中微子质量，精度在无形状噪声时达0.096 eV，Stage-III级噪声下为0.340 eV，并验证了该信号与中微子质量呈线性关系及正向建模的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙空洞作为大尺度结构中的低密度区域，提供与高密度区互补的宇宙学信息；中微子质量是当前宇宙学关键未解问题之一，亟需新探针进行独立约束。

Method: 基于不同中微子质量的宇宙学模拟，使用DIVE空洞探测器识别空洞，结合暗物质与中微子分布获取密度剖面；通过光线追踪生成模拟剪切星表，测量空洞透镜信号；并开展正向建模验证。

Result: 空洞透镜信号在无形状噪声下对总中微子质量的约束精度为σ(M_ν)=0.096 eV，在Stage-III类形状噪声（σ_e ≃ 0.3）下为σ(M_ν)=0.340 eV；发现该信号与中微子质量呈清晰线性关系；正向建模在不同宇宙学模型下均准确可靠。

Conclusion: 空洞透镜效应是一种有前景的中微子质量探针，值得应用于实际星系巡天数据，并与其他宇宙学观测联合分析。

Abstract: Cosmic voids, the underdense regions of the Large Scale Structure (LSS), provide cosmological information highly complementary to that obtained from overdense regions. In this work, we investigate the constraining power of the void-shear cross-correlation (void lensing effect) on the total neutrino mass. Based on cosmological simulations with varying neutrino masses, we identify voids with the DIVE void finder and obtain their density profiles from the underlying dark matter and neutrino distributions. We then generate mock shear catalogues through ray-tracing and measure the corresponding void lensing signals. Our results show that void lensing yields an independent constraint on total neutrino mass as $σ(M_ν)=0.096\,{\rm eV}$ in the absence of shape noise, and $σ(M_ν)=0.340\,{\rm eV}$ when adopting a Stage-III-like shape noise ($σ_e \simeq 0.3$). Moreover, we find a clear linear relationship between the void lensing signal and neutrino mass. We further validate the forward modelling of the void lensing signal from the void density profiles across different cosmologies, demonstrating its accuracy and potential for future applications. These findings highlight void lensing as a promising probe of massive neutrinos and motivate its applications to galaxy survey data as well as the combination with other cosmological observables.

</details>


### [9] [Mock Catalogs of Strongly Lensed Gravitational Waves via A Halo Model Approach with Ground-based Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09289)
*Youkai Li,Kai Liao,Mingqi Sun,Lilan Yang,Xuheng Ding,Marek Biesiada,Tonghua Liu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个包含暗物质晕、星系和子晕的复合透镜质量模型，生成了强引力波透镜事件的模拟星表，并预测了第三代探测器（如ET+CE）每年可探测到约400个双像、36个四像事件，其中包含约107个子晕透镜事件和20个可观测中心像的完整三/五像系统；同时分析了高放大率事件及不同模型对事件率的影响，为未来引力波透镜信号识别提供了更可靠的统计先验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着第三代引力波探测器建设推进，强引力波透镜事件的探测日益重要，亟需基于物理更自洽的模型预测其统计特征与可观测性。

Method: 构建融合暗物质晕、星系及子晕的复合透镜质量模型，生成多源种群、多种探测器组网（含地球自转效应）下的强引力波透镜模拟星表，涵盖双像、四像、子晕透镜、高放大率及含可观测中心像的三/五像系统，并系统分析事件率、信噪比对分布与时间延迟等统计特性。

Result: 预测ET+CE联合网络年探测率约为400个双像、36个四像事件，含约107个子晕透镜事件、20个含可观测中心像的完整系统，以及约360个高放大率（μ>3）事件；放宽探测条件后总透镜事件达约617个；并量化了透镜质量模型与恒星演化模型对结果的影响。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了迄今最全面、物理更真实的强引力波透镜模拟星表（GW-LMC），建立了更可靠的统计先验，支撑未来透镜信号的识别、验证与天体物理应用。

Abstract: As plans for the construction of third-generation gravitational wave (GW) detectors advance, research into strongly lensed GWs has become increasingly critical. It is anticipated that hundreds of multi-image lensed GWs will be detected annually. We present a comprehensive suite of lensed GW mock catalog derived from a composite lens mass model incorporating dark matter halos, galaxies, and subhalos. We analyze three source populations with four detector network configurations considering the earth rotation. Our simulations encompass not only conventional doublets and quadruplets but also subhalo-lensed events, highly magnified systems, and complete three or five image systems with a detectable central image, a feature distinct from optical lensing. For the joint ET+CE network, we forecast an annual detection rate of approximately 400 doublets and 36 quadruplets. Notably, this population includes roughly 107 events lensed by subhalos and 20 complete systems with detectable central images. Furthermore, we analyze high-magnification events ($μ> 3$), predicting approximately 360 such cases. Under a more relaxed selection criterion that requires only at least one lensed signal to exceed the detection threshold, we estimate a total of approximately 617 lensed events. We also investigate the impact of variations in lens mass models and stellar evolution models on event rates, as well as the distributions of SNR pairs and time delays. These results establish a more physically grounded statistical prior for the future identification and authentication of lensed GW signals. The Gravitational Waves-Lensing Mock Catalog (GW-LMC) have been made publicly available.

</details>


### [10] [Reliable Tests of Faint-end UV Luminosity Functions in Strong Lensing Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09308)
*Jiashuo Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过强引力透镜效应探测超轻暗物质（ψDM）模型在高红移星系光度函数暗端的截断特征，发现现有测光红移样本中存在大量低红移污染，并提出结合HST/JWST观测和机器学习方法进行有效剔除；最终在MACS J0416场中未观测到截断，从而对ψDM质量给出95%置信下限：>2.97×10⁻²² eV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验两种主流暗物质模型——传统重粒子模型与超轻玻色子暗物质（ψDM，质量约10⁻²² eV）模型，尤其关注ψDM预言的高红移星系光度函数暗端截断特征。

Method: 利用大质量星系团的强引力透镜放大效应探测更暗、更高红移的星系；分析并量化低红移星系对高红移样本的污染；结合HST与JWST深度成像数据及机器学习方法剔除红移误判；构建更干净的3.5≤z≤5.5和6≤z≤10星系样本，在MACS J0416场中统计光度函数。

Result: 发现HFF测光红移目录中约50%标为3.5≤z≤5.5的星系实为低红移污染物；通过数据融合与机器学习显著提升样本纯度；在MACS J0416中未探测到ψDM预期的光度函数暗端截断；由此给出ψDM粒子质量95%置信下限为2.97×10⁻²² eV。

Conclusion: 当前观测不支持极轻质量ψDM主导暗物质，所得质量下限反映其德布罗意尺度对整体暗物质分布的集体引力约束；该结果亦适用于多组分ψDM模型，其有效质量由整体引力平衡决定。

Abstract: Dark matter comprises ~85% of the entire mass of the Universe, but the fundamental nature of its constituent particles remains elusive. In this thesis, I test for two competitive dark matter models: the conventional heavy particle paradigm, and dark matter being ultralight bosons of mass $\sim 10^{-22}$eV ($ψ$DM). More specifically, I test for the faint-end turnover induced by $ψ$DM models, exploiting the strong lensing power by massive galaxy clusters to probe intrinsically fainter magnitudes. A key challenge for such an analysis would be contamination by low-z galaxies sharing similar observed SEDs as high-z galaxies. As I will demonstrate, such a contamination issue is generally severe and may wash out the faint-end turnover signatures. I also show that $\sim 50\%$ of the purported $3.5\leq z\leq 5.5$ galaxies within existing photometric redshift catalogs constructed for Hubble Frontier Fields (HFF) are in fact low-z interlopers. Luckily, individual mitigation of interlopers can be achieved with the combination of deep HST and JWST observations. For fields without supplementary data, machine learning methods will be shown useful in preserving the mitigating power. Cleaner $3.5\leq z\leq 5.5$ and $6\leq z\leq 10$ samples are derived for a more reliable test in strong lensing field of MACS J0416, with which I found no evidence for faint-end turnovers, leading to a constraint on the $ψ$DM mass of $>2.97\times10^{-22}$eV at 95\% confidence. This constraint will also be interpreted in an scheme where dark matter is composed of multiple particle copies, where I argue the derived mass bound is likely on an effective de Broglie scale governing the collective behavior of the entire $ψ$DM budget under gravitational equilibrium established.

</details>


### [11] [Hidden Vela Supercluster Revealed by First Hybrid Redshift & Peculiar Velocity Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09339)
*A. M. Hollinger,H. M. Courtois,R. C. Kraan-Korteweg,J. Mould,S. H. A. Rajohnson*

Method: 融合CF4++星系本动速度数据（65518个）与新获取的8283个南银道面（|b|≤10°）红移数据，其中包含2176个利用MeerKAT望远镜获得的高灵敏度HI干涉红移，首次覆盖南ZOA最内侧3度宽条带并达到前所未有的深度。

Conclusion: 该混合重建方法提供了迄今最完整、动力学自洽的南ZOA图像，验证了其在下一代大尺度巡天中的变革性潜力。

Abstract: A large fraction of the extragalactic sky is obscured by foreground dust and stars along the plane of the Milky Way, leaving a major gap (~ 20%) in whole-sky maps of large-scale structures -- an incompleteness that is even more severe for peculiar velocity samples. This has long limited an unambiguous interpretation of observed cosmic flows and their connection to the underlying mass-density field.
  We present a new hybrid reconstruction methodology which combines 65,518 galaxy peculiar velocity distances from the CF4++ catalogue (Courtois2025) with 8283 new galaxy redshifts observed near the southern Galactic plane (|b| <= 10 degrees) Zone of Avoidance. A major advance is the inclusion of 2176 high-sensitivity, interferometric HI redshifts obtained with the SARAO MeerKAT telescope which for the first time provide coverage of the innermost 3degrees-wide strip of the southern ZOA and to unprecedented depth.
  This hybrid redshifts & peculiar velocities approach yields a substantially revised view of the inferred overdensities in and around the ZOA. In particular, the Vela supercluster emerges as a dominant mass concentration, rivaling the Shapley concentration and exceeding the mass associated with Laniakea and the Great Attractor region. With a total mass of 33.8 10^16 Msol, a characteristic radius of 70 hmpc, and a double core morphology at a distance of 189 hmpc, Vela dominates the mass budget and gravitational influence of the southern Zone of Avoidance. These results provide the most complete and dynamically consistent picture to date of the southern Zone of Avoidance and demonstrate the transformative potential of hybrid reconstruction techniques tailored for the next generation of large-scale surveys.

### [13] [Exploring the $S_8$ Tension: Insights from the CatNorth 1.5-Million Quasar Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09457)
*Jin Qin,Xue-Bing Wu,Yuming Fu,Haojie Xu,Yuxuan Pang,Yun-Hao Zhang,Pengjie Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用CatNorth 150万个类星体候选体样本与Planck DR4 CMB透镜数据，通过自相关和互相关分析测量结构增长参数S8，发现低红移（z<1.5）结果S8=0.844±0.057与Planck CMB一致，缓解了以往弱引力透镜与CMB之间的~3σ张力；高红移（z>1.5）结果偏低可能源于样本不完备或前景污染。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决宇宙学中S8参数在高红移（CMB）与低红移（弱引力透镜）观测之间存在的约3σ张力，判断其源于系统误差还是新物理。

Method: 使用CatNorth类星体候选体目录与Planck DR4 CMB透镜数据，开展自相关与交叉相关分析；针对空间不完备性，构建基于机器学习的选源函数以压制大尺度系统性功率谱偏差。

Result: 低红移（z<1.5）测得S8 = 0.844^{+0.058}_{-0.056}，与Planck 2018 CMB结果（0.834±0.016）一致；高红移（z>1.5）结果偏低（如0.724±0.056），体积限制样本也显示S8随红移升高而下降的趋势。

Conclusion: 基于大样本类星体的新测量表明S8张力显著减弱，支持ΛCDM框架下系统误差主导该张力，而非新物理；高红移结果偏低需进一步排除样本不完备与前景污染影响。

Abstract: The parameter $S_8$, a key probe of cosmic structure growth, exhibits a persistent $\sim3σ$ tension between high-redshift measurements from cosmic microwave background (CMB) anisotropies and low-redshift weak gravitational lensing observations. This discrepancy may indicate either unaccounted systematic effects or new physics beyond the standard $Λ$CDM cosmology. In this work, we constrain $S_8$ using the high purity CatNorth 1.5 million quasar candidate catalog and the {\it Planck} DR4 CMB lensing data across the broad redshift ranges through auto-correlation and cross-correlation analyses. To address the spatial incompleteness, we develop a machine-learning-based selection function that effectively suppresses the systematics-induced power spectrum excess on large scales. Our robust low-redshift measurements at $z<1.5$ yield $S_8 = 0.844^{+0.058}_{-0.056}$, consistent with the {\it Planck} 2018 CMB anisotropies constraints of $S_8=0.834\pm0.016$ but lower than the $0.879^{+0.055}_{-0.055}$ reported by a previous work using the Quaia quasar candidate catalog. However, for high-redshift faint quasars at $z>1.5$, we find a lower value of $S_8=0.724^{+0.058}_{-0.054}$, likely due to the sample incompleteness and/or the foreground contamination. Further tests on the volume-limited samples exhibit a consistent trend: $S_8 = 0.835^{+0.053}_{-0.049}$ for $z < 2$, $0.824^{+0.061}_{-0.062}$ for $0.4 < z < 1.5$, and a lower value of $0.789^{+0.062}_{-0.062}$ for the higher redshift range of $1.5 < z < 2.5$. While future data may refine these results, our current measurements based on a large sample of quasar candidates show less evidence of the $S_8$ tension.

### [14] [Dark Matter Recoupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09969)
*Eugenia Dallari,Francesco Castagna,Emanuele Castorina,Maria Archidiacono,Ennio Salvioni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种暗物质'再耦合'新机制：暗物质在早期弱相互作用，但在宇宙晚期（如星系巡天所探查的红移范围内）与暗辐射重新耦合，导致相互作用显著增强；CMB和BAO数据限制了当前整体暗物质的相互作用强度，但允许约4%的暗物质成分至今仍强相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战传统上将暗物质视为全程碰撞less的假设，探索其相互作用随宇宙演化而增强的可能性，以调和理论预期与观测约束。

Method: 系统研究暗物质与暗辐射在晚期宇宙中再耦合的唯象学，结合CMB和BAO观测数据对相互作用强度进行限制，并讨论微观模型实现路径。

Result: 发现若全部暗物质参与再耦合，则当前相互作用必须很弱；但允许约4%的暗物质成分至今仍可强相互作用；该机制自然满足早期CMB约束，同时在晚期产生可观测效应。

Conclusion: 暗物质相互作用可具有显著的时间演化性，晚期再耦合是一种可行且尚未被充分探索的新物理图景，为暗物质性质研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: In the late Universe, and on cosmological scales, dark matter is conventionally assumed to be collisionless, as a consequence of the strong existing bounds on dark matter interactions at the Cosmic Microwave Background last-scattering surface. Challenging this lore, here we show that dark matter interactions can be naturally weak at early times, but then grow to observationally relevant strengths at very late times, even significantly after reionization. This is realized if dark matter recouples to a dark radiation species in the range of redshifts probed by the current generation of galaxy surveys. We systematically study, for the first time, the phenomenology of this dark matter recoupling scenario. A combination of Cosmic Microwave Background and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation data show that the interaction needs to be weak at present, if the entirety of dark matter couples to dark radiation. From a complementary perspective, a 4% fraction of dark matter could still be strongly interacting today. Implications for a microscopic model realizing the recoupling dynamics are discussed.

</details>


### [15] [Probing Physics Beyond the Standard Model through Combined Analyses of Next-Generation Type Ia Supernova, CMB, and BAO Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09973)
*Srinivasan Raghunathan,Ayan Mitra,Nikolina Šarčević,Fei Ge,Corentin Ravoux,Christos Georgiou,Renée Hložek,Richard Kessler,Gautham Narayan,Paul Rogozenski,Paul Shah,Georgios Valogiannis,Joaquin Vieira,the LSST Dark Energy Science Collaboration*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过结合LSST的Ia型超新星（SNIa）、DESI的BAO以及多个CMB实验（SPT、SO、CMB-S4）数据，对未来暗能量参数（w0, wa）和中微子质量总和（∑mν）的观测约束进行了预测。结果表明，LSST-Y3+SNIa+DESI-DR3+CM B联合分析可将w0和wa的误差分别降至0.028和0.11，并有望实现2–3σ水平的∑mν探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用多时代宇宙学探针（SNIa、BAO、CMB）的互补性，提升对暗能量状态方程和中微子质量等关键宇宙学参数的限制精度，检验ΛCDM及其扩展模型。

Method: 采用Markov Chain Monte Carlo（MCMC）采样框架，联合模拟LSST Year-3 SNIa样本、DESI DR3 BAO数据及多个CMB实验（含TT/EE/TE/φφ谱）的观测信息，对ΛCDM、w0waCDM及含∑mν和空间曲率的扩展模型进行参数估计。

Result: LSST-Y3 SNIa比DES Y5将w0、wa约束提升2–2.5倍；DESI DR3比DR2提升达1.8倍；三者联合给出σ(w0)=0.028、σ(wa)=0.11；自由化∑mν和曲率使约束弱化10%–30%；联合分析可实现2–3σ的∑mν探测。

Conclusion: LSST、DESI与下一代CMB实验的协同观测将显著增强对暗能量演化及中微子质量的限制能力，为超越ΛCDM模型提供关键检验手段。

Abstract: Observations of Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and the cosmic microwave background (CMB), which probe the late-, intermediate-, and early-universe epochs, respectively, provide complementary constraints on the expansion history of the Universe. In this work, we forecast constraints on dark energy and other extensions to the standard cosmological model by combining the SNIa sample expected from the Vera C. Rubin Observatory's Legacy Survey of Space and Time (LSST), data from current and forthcoming CMB surveys, and BAO measurements from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI). For the CMB, we use temperature, polarization, and lensing power spectra ($TT/EE/TE/φφ$) from South Pole Telescope, the planned Advanced Simons Observatory, and a CMB-S4-like experiment. We derive constraints on $Λ{\rm CDM}$ and its extensions involving the dark energy equation of state parameters $(w_{0}, w_{a})$ and the sum of neutrino masses $\sum m_ν$, using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) sampling framework. We find that the LSST Year-3 SNIa sample can improve upon the DES Year-5 dark energy constraints by a factor of $\times2-\times2.5$, with the gains driven primarily by the significantly higher SNIa density in the LSST sample. Similarly, DESI-DR3 shows up to a $\times1.8$ improvement on dark energy parameters over DR2, driven largely by the substantial increase in low-redshift sample. Combining CMB with LSST-Y3-SNIa and DESI-DR3-BAO yields $σ(w_{0}) = 0.028$ and $σ(w_{a}) = 0.11$ for $w_{0} w_{a} {\rm CDM}$ cosmology with the results being largely independent of the CMB dataset. The constraints weaken by 10%-30% when freeing $\sum m_ν$ and spatial curvature. Moreover, the joint analysis of the three datasets can enable a $2-3σ$ detection of $\sum m_ν$.

</details>

### [16] [Thermodynamics and Optical Properties of Charged Black Holes in Bumblebee gravity Sourced by a Cloud of Strings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08764)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Shubham Kala,Ahmad Al-Badawi*

TL;DR: 本文研究了bumblebee引力理论中带有弦云的静态球对称带电黑洞解，分析了其热力学、光学性质及太阳系内的经典引力检验，以探索洛伦兹破缺对广义相对论的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在洛伦兹对称性自发破缺的引力理论中，非最小耦合的bumblebee矢量场获得非零真空期望值，从而修改标准广义相对论；本文旨在探究此类理论中带弦云的黑洞解及其可观测效应。

Method: 通过求解bumblebee引力场方程得到静态球对称带电黑洞解，系统分析其热力学（质量、温度、熵）、光学性质（光子球、黑洞阴影、光线偏折）以及太阳系内经典检验（如近日点进动）。

Abstract: In theories where the Lorentz symmetry of gravity is spontaneously broken, a non-minimally coupled bumblebee vector field acquires a nonzero vacuum expectation value, leading to modifications of standard General Relativity (GR). In this work, we investigate exact solutions describing static and spherically symmetric charged black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings within the framework of bumblebee gravity. We begin by analyzing the thermodynamic properties of these black hole solutions, including their mass, temperature, and entropy, highlighting how Lorentz-violating effects alter standard results. Next, we examine the optical properties of the spacetime, focusing on the photon sphere, the resulting black hole shadow, and the deflection of light, thereby providing potential observational signatures of Lorentz violation. Finally, we explore the impact of Lorentz-violating parameters on classical gravitational tests within the Solar System, such as advance of perihelion precession, in order to set observational constraints. Our analysis provides a comprehensive investigation of the interplay between Lorentz violation, black hole physics, and cloud of strings, offering a framework to probe new physics beyond GR.

### [17] [Singular gauge transformations in geometrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08766)
*Alcides Garat*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦时空中的非零电磁场新四标架与局部电磁规范变换群之间的直接联系，研究了能将类时-类空平面中的向量映射到该平面与局部光锥交集的奇异局域规范变换的存在性与几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立新四标架与局部电磁规范变换群之间的直接联系，并研究特定奇异规范变换的存在性及其几何意义。

Method: 基于先前为非零电磁场引入的新四标架，分析其构造特点，探讨其与爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦应力-能量张量本征向量平面相关的局部四标架变换群及规范依赖性。

Result: 发现存在能将类时和类空向量映射到类时-类空平面与局部光锥交集的奇异局域规范变换，并需对其数学结构与几何特性进行刻画。

Conclusion: 新四标架提供了连接电磁规范自由度与时空几何结构的新途径，奇异规范变换的识别对理解其物理与几何含义至关重要。

Abstract: The new tetrads introduced previously for non-null electromagnetic fields in Einstein- Maxwell spacetimes enable a direct link to the local electromagnetic gauge group of transformations. Due to the peculiar elements in the construction of these new tetrads a direct connection can be established between the local group of electromagnetic gauge transformations and local groups of tetrad transformations on two different local and orthogonal planes of eigenvectors of the Einstein-Maxwell stress-energy tensor. These tetrad vectors are gauge dependent. It is an interesting and relevant problem to study if there are local gauge transformations that can map on the timelike-spacelike plane, the timelike and the spacelike vectors into the intersection of the local light cone and the plane itself. How many of these local gauge transformations exist and how the mathematics and the geometry of these particular transformations play out. These local gauge transformations would be singular and it is important to identify them.

### [18] [Spin Induced Geometry: Emergence of Metric and Torsional Sectors from Spinor Source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08769)
*Elisa Varani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一个几何框架，其中度规和挠率自由度均从自旋流中动态涌现，而非作为仿射联络的基本属性被预先设定；基本动力学变量是一个携带局域洛伦兹指标的三阶场，满足由费米子自旋流驱动的质量型Klein-Gordon方程；其时空投影给出非对称二阶张量，对称与反对称部分分别对应自旋诱导的有效度规与传播性挠率；二者均具质量并呈Yukawa压制，从而在长程引力中解耦；不同于Einstein-Cartan理论，此处挠率为传播型；自旋less粒子沿该有效度规测地线运动，因而间接感知自旋流；三种费米子（Dirac、Weyl、Majorana）对应不同几何相，在Majorana极限下几何纯为轴向挠率型，并支持涡旋与类Skyrmion等拓扑非平庸构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 克服传统引力理论（如广义相对论和Einstein-Cartan理论）中度规与挠率需人为预设、且挠率不传播或不产生间接自旋效应的局限，探索几何结构完全由自旋流动力学生成的可能性。

Method: 引入一个携带局域洛伦兹指标的三阶场作为基本变量，导出其满足的质量型Klein-Gordon方程，分析其时空投影的对称/反对称分解，推导有效度规与挠率的动力学性质，并系统比较Dirac、Weyl、Majorana费米子作为源所导致的几何响应差异。

Result: 成功构建一个度规与挠率均从自旋流动态涌现的几何框架；证明挠率为传播型且质量化；揭示自旋less粒子可通过有效度规间接响应自旋流；在Majorana极限下获得轴向挠率主导的拓扑几何结构（如涡旋、Skyrmion）。

Conclusion: 几何并非先验背景，而是费米子自旋流的动力学产物；该框架统一处理度规与挠率起源，拓展了自旋-几何耦合的物理内涵，并为量子引力中的拓扑几何激发提供新机制。

Abstract: We present a geometric framework in which both metric and torsional degrees of freedom emerge dynamically from spinor currents, without being postulated as fundamental properties of the affine connection. The fundamental dynamical variable is a rank-three field carrying local Lorentz indices, governed by a massive Klein--Gordon equation sourced by fermionic spin currents. Its projection onto spacetime indices yields a rank-two tensor with no definite symmetry; the symmetric and antisymmetric sectors define, respectively, an effective spin-induced metric and the torsional degrees of freedom. Both sectors are massive and Yukawa-suppressed, ensuring decoupling from long-range gravitational dynamics. Unlike Einstein--Cartan theory, torsion here is propagating rather than algebraically constrained. A key consequence is that spinless test particles follow geodesics of the effective metric and are therefore indirectly sensitive to spin currents through the emergent geometric structure~ -- ~a mechanism absent in both standard General Relativity and Einstein--Cartan theory. The spinorial structure of the source is analyzed across three regimes: general Dirac, Weyl, and Majorana fermions, each giving rise to a distinct geometric phase. In the Majorana limit, the geometry becomes purely axial-torsional, admitting topologically non-trivial configurations such as vortices and Skyrmion-like structures, which emerge dynamically from the spinorial source.

### [19] [Partial Orderings of Curvature Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08775)
*Ivica Smolić*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文建立了新的点态不等式，用于在不同Petrov和Segre类型的时空中对曲率不变量进行排序，并系统分析了任意维度时空中Ricci张量收缩之间的不等式关系，同时探讨了(1+3)维时空中Zakhary-McIntosh不变量被Kretschmann标量控制的条件，从而构建了曲率标量的实用层级结构。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立点态不等式，系统分析Ricci张量的各种收缩形式，并研究Zakhary-McIntosh不变量与Kretschmann标量之间的上界关系。

Result: 得到了适用于任意维度及特定(1+3)维时空的曲率不变量排序不等式，明确了高阶不变量如何被低阶不变量代数控制。

Conclusion: 曲率标量之间存在可实用的层级结构，高阶曲率不变量在一定条件下可由低阶不变量（如Kretschmann标量）控制。

Abstract: We establish a new set of pointwise inequalities that order curvature invariants across various Petrov and Segre types of spacetimes. In arbitrary spacetime dimension, we systematically analyze inequalities among contractions of the Ricci tensor. We further explore the conditions under which all Zakhary--McIntosh invariants in $(1+3)$-dimensional spacetimes are bounded above (up to appropriate powers) by the Kretschmann scalar. These results establish a practical hierarchy among curvature scalars and clarify the extent to which higher-order invariants are algebraically controlled by lower-order ones or vice versa.

### [20] [Strong-deflection expansion of the deflection angle near a degenerate photon sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08778)
*Takahisa Igata,Tadashi Sasaki,Naoki Tsukamoto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个强偏转展开式，用于计算在渐近平直、静态、球对称时空中的退化光子球附近散射的光线偏转角；该方法能明确分离出在临界轨道附近产生的发散贡献，并给出唯一主导幂律项；主导系数可分解为普适常数与由有效势三阶导数决定的局域因子，并进一步用Weyl张量电部分构造的潮汐量及其在广义相对论中与加权零能量密度的关系予以几何解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统强偏转极限方法在光子球退化（即边际轨道）情形下难以保持良好定义，本文旨在建立一种在退化极限下仍保持明确定义且具物理可解性的偏转角展开框架。

Method: 基于渐近平直、静态、球对称时空度规，对光线偏转角积分实施强偏转展开；通过精细分离被积函数在退化光子球附近的奇异性，提取出在最近接近半径和冲击参数两种展开下的主导发散项；引入Weyl张量电部分构造无量纲潮汐量，并分析其面积半径导数的几何意义。

Result: 获得偏转角在退化光子球附近的唯一主导幂律形式；证明主导系数在最近接近半径展开下可因子化为普适常数与局域第三阶有效势导数的乘积；该局域因子具有由Weyl电部分定义的不变几何表达；在广义相对论中进一步关联到加权零能量密度的径向导数；多个解析例子验证了该因子化结构并给出闭式发散系数。

Conclusion: 本文提出的强偏转展开方法在退化光子球极限下保持良好定义且具普适性与几何清晰性，为研究极端致密天体（如临界黑洞或超紧凑星）的强引力透镜效应提供了新工具，并揭示了偏转行为与时空局部曲率及能量分布的深层联系。

Abstract: We present a strong-deflection expansion for the deflection angle of light rays scattered near a degenerate photon sphere in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. Our prescription isolates the divergent contribution to the deflection-angle integral arising from the ray's passage near the marginal orbit in a way that remains well defined at marginality, thereby yielding a unique leading power-law term. When expressed in terms of the radius of closest approach, the leading coefficient in the strong deflection limit factorizes into a universal branch constant and a local factor determined by the third derivative of the effective potential at the degenerate photon sphere. Passing to the expansion in terms of the impact parameter then only multiplies the coefficient by an additional local conversion factor. We show that the local factor in the closest-approach expansion admits an invariant representation through the areal-radius derivative of a dimensionless tidal measure constructed from the electric part of the Weyl tensor. In general relativity, we further relate this quantity to the areal-radius derivative of a weighted null-energy density profile. Analytic examples validate this factorization and yield closed-form expressions for the leading divergent coefficients in representative marginal configurations.

### [21] [Scalar shortcut to beyond-Kerr ringdown tests and their complementarity with black-hole shadow observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08782)
*Paolo Pani,Andrea P. Sanna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过计算标量场在黑洞背景下的准正规模（QNMs）及其相对于广义相对论预测的偏差，来近似估计引力场QNMs修正的新方法；该方法在Kerr-Newman和Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet黑洞中精度达数十个百分点，优于或至少媲美传统eikonal近似，并被成功应用于现象学度规，给出与黑洞阴影观测相当甚至更强的ringdown约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统eikonal近似虽方便但精度有限，尤其在低角动量区域；亟需一种更可靠、易实施的近似策略来估算新物理模型中引力准正规模的修正。

Method: 精确计算测试标量场在各类黑洞背景（包括Kerr-Newman、Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet及多种现象学度规）中的准正规模，将其偏离广义相对论预言的偏差作为引力模式修正的代理；不依赖eikonal极限，亦无需完整引力扰动方程求解。

Result: 该标量代理法在具体理论模型中重现引力QNMs修正的精度达~10–30%；对当前百分比精度的ringdown测量已足够；在部分现象学度规中，所得ringdown约束强于或等价于黑洞阴影观测，且覆盖后者无法探测的参数空间。

Conclusion: 标量场准正规模的偏差可作为引力模式修正的有效、高性价比代理；该方法兼具理论简洁性与实际约束力，为多信使引力检验提供了新范式。

Abstract: The quasinormal modes of black holes (BHs) in the large-angular-momentum limit can be computed within the eikonal approximation. This approximation is often extrapolated to low angular momentum to obtain a rough estimate of the dominant ringdown modes. Although approximate, this approach is particularly convenient in theories beyond general relativity with intricate dynamics, or for phenomenological metrics that lack an underlying fundamental theory. Here we explore a complementary approximate strategy: we compute exactly the quasinormal modes of a test scalar field propagating on the BH background and use their \emph{deviations} from the general-relativity predictions as a proxy for the corresponding corrections to the gravitational quasinormal modes. For Kerr-Newman and Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet BHs, we show that this method reproduces the exact corrections (including the coupling among different degrees of freedom) within tens of percent, an accuracy that is adequate as long as ringdown measurements remain at the percent level. Furthermore, this method is typically comparable to, or more accurate than, the eikonal approximation. We then apply the same strategy to phenomenological metrics commonly employed in tests of gravity using BH imaging. By computing scalar quasinormal modes in a large family of these metrics for the first time, we find that current ringdown constraints are comparable to, and in some cases more stringent than, those derived from BH shadow observations, while also providing complementary bounds on sectors that would otherwise be inaccessible.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文研究了克尔黑洞光子环在相空间中的自相似结构及其动力学行为，揭示了在接近束缚光子轨道时由李雅普诺夫指数控制的动力学特性，并指出当时空偏离克尔几何时混沌现象开始出现，尤其在光子壳层中强共振束缚轨道附近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞光子环在相空间中的结构及其对时空几何变化的响应，特别是混沌行为如何随背景时空变形而产生。

Method: 通过分析光子壳层附近的动力学，计算近束缚光线的首返映射，并研究时空偏离克尔几何时混沌的出现机制。

Result: 发现光子环的自相似结构在相空间中依然存在；近束缚光线虽具指数敏感性但不混沌；时空变形后混沌在强共振束缚轨道附近率先出现，并形成分形相空间结构。

Conclusion: 光子环的自相似性与相空间分形结构紧密关联，混沌的 onset 揭示了黑洞阴影观测中潜在的非线性动力学特征，为未来高分辨率观测提供理论依据。

Abstract: The photon ring of a Kerr black hole decomposes into a self-similar hierarchy of subrings. Here, we show that this self-similar structure persists in phase space. Moreover, near the photon shell of bound photon orbits, dynamics are controlled by a Lyapunov exponent $γ$, whose role we highlight by computing the first-return map for light rays close to an unstably bound orbit. Despite an exponential $e^γ$ sensitivity to initial conditions, nearly bound rays do not exhibit chaotic behavior. However, as the background spacetime is deformed away from the Kerr geometry, chaos sets in, with its first onset most visible near strongly resonant bound orbits in the photon shell. We display two animations: one illustrating the emergence of chaos near the photon shell, which results in a fractal phase-space structure, and another exhibiting how this chaotic, fractal, self-similar structure is encoded in the first-return map.

### [23] [Inspirals into bosonic dark matter stars and chirp mimickers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08795)
*Caio F. B. Macedo,Haroldo C. D. Lima,Raissa F. P. Mendes,Rodrigo Vicente,Vitor Cardoso*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索玻色子星作为黑洞替代模型的可能性，检验其是否能在引力波观测中模拟黑洞双星信号，从而为暗物质本质和致密天体物理提供新约束。

Method: 采用全相对论性微扰方法，建模恒星质量致密天体绕超大质量玻色子星的极端质量比旋进，并推导引力波与标量波的能量通量半解析公式。

Result: 发现动力学摩擦导致的标量物质辐射可显著改变旋进动力学，产生类啁啾引力波信号；高致密玻色子星激发偶极标量辐射引发快速并合，低致密情形则以四极标量波与引力波为主；所提能量通量公式在强场下仍保持高精度。

Conclusion: 玻色子星即使非超致密亦可模仿黑洞引力波啁啾信号，但其相位演化因标量耗散而存在可观测偏差，未来LISA等探测器有望据此区分真实黑洞与玻色子星模型。

Abstract: We investigate extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in which a stellar-mass compact object orbits a supermassive bosonic dark matter star, modeled as a boson star, using fully relativistic perturbative methods. Unlike inspirals around electro-vacuum black holes, these systems can shed scalar matter through dynamical friction which significantly alters the inspiral dynamics. We show that this additional dissipation can induce a chirp-like gravitational-wave signal closely resembling that of black hole binaries, allowing boson stars to act as gravitational-wave chirp mimickers even when they are not ultracompact. The inspiral evolution and resulting waveform depend sensitively on the compactness of the central boson star: highly compact configurations trigger dipolar scalar radiation, leading to a rapid plunge, whereas less compact stars yield smoother inspirals dominated by gravitational and quadrupolar scalar waves. To support waveform modeling, we derive semi-analytical prescriptions for the gravitational and scalar energy fluxes that remain accurate deep into the relativistic regime. Our findings indicate that future space-based detectors such as LISA could distinguish these mimicker signals from true black hole inspirals through measurable phase dephasings induced by scalar dissipation.

### [24] [Images of the Thin Accretion Disk Around Kerr Black Holes coupled to time periodic scalar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08796)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合类时圆轨道分析与后向光线追踪方法，研究带有两个时间周期性标量场的旋转Kerr黑洞的测地结构和薄Novikov-Thorne吸积盘的发射特性。

Result: 标量电荷归一化值主导正向与逆向吸积盘的形态和亮度；强标量化下出现额外光圈和修改后的圆轨道区，导致多个内辐射区和显著增强的红移模式；逆向盘尤为敏感，产生高亮且具独特频移特征的内逆行辐射环。

Abstract: We investigate the orbital structure and observable appearance of rotating Kerr black holes endowed with synchronized scalar hair described by two time-periodic scalar fields with a flat target-space geometry. The presence of scalar hair enriches the geodesic structure of the spacetime relative to the Kerr case and significantly modifies the emission properties of geometrically thin Novikov-Thorne accretion disks. Combining an analysis of timelike circular orbits with backward ray tracing, we show that the normalized scalar charge governs the morphology and luminosity of both prograde and counter-rotating disks. In the strongly scalarized regime, additional light rings and modified circular-orbit regions produce multiple inner emitting zones and strongly enhanced redshift patterns that depart markedly from the Kerr prediction. The most pronounced deviations occur in the counter-rotating sector, where scalar hair generates inner retrograde radiative rings with substantially enhanced luminosity and distinctive frequency-shift signatures. Even when the spacetime approaches the Kerr geometry at weaker scalarization, the retrograde disk remains highly sensitive to the presence of scalar hair. Our results demonstrate that geometrically thin accretion disks can provide robust observational diagnostics of synchronized scalar hair and may offer a promising avenue for testing tensor-multi-scalar gravity with future horizon-scale black-hole imaging observations.

### [25] [Extreme mass ratio head-on collisions of black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.08839)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索修正引力理论（特别是Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet引力）中黑洞并合事件视界演化的特征，检验等效原理和标量场对光子传播及并合动力学的影响；扩展无限质量比近似方法至带发黑洞场景。

Method: 采用光线追踪技术，在单个带发黑洞时空背景下模拟无限质量比近似下的头对头碰撞；分析三种标量场耦合函数（线性、二次、特定指数形式）对应的静态黑洞性质与光子环结构；计算并合持续时间与视界面积增量，并与广义相对论及已有数值模拟结果对比。

Result: 三种耦合下，小黑洞尺寸固定且耦合常数较小时，并合持续时间均长于广义相对论；但指数耦合在足够大的耦合常数下呈现非单调行为，并合时间可短于GR；并合持续时间与面积增量普遍跟随小黑洞光子环行为；结果与部分数值模拟趋势一致。

Conclusion: 光子环是刻画带发黑洞并合动力学的关键几何特征；Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet理论中，标量场耦合形式显著影响并合时标，尤其指数耦合可能导致反直觉的加速并合现象，为引力波观测提供潜在新信号特征。

Abstract: The evolution of the event horizon when two black holes merge can be determined by resorting to ray-tracing techniques on a single black hole spacetime, under the assumption that the binary's mass ratio is infinite and the underlying gravity theory respects the equivalence principle. We extend this analysis to the head-on collision of non-spinning hairy black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In such theories the scalar field is coupled to a higher curvature operator, leading to possible modifications of the background geometry and consequently of photon propagation. We study three families of coupling functions: linear, quadratic, and a particular exponential form. The first choice enjoys a shift symmetry and forces the presence of scalar hair in the spectrum of black hole solutions. The latter two couplings break the shift symmetry and allow for spontaneously scalarized hairy black holes, which coexist with the Schwarzschild black hole. For all three classes of theories studied, we find a merger duration that is longer than the corresponding time in general relativity, when keeping the size of the small black hole fixed, and for viably small values of the coupling constant. However, the case of the exponential coupling yields a non-monotonic merger duration, which can become shorter than the general relativity value for a sufficiently large coupling constant. We observe that the merger duration and the area increment generically track the behavior of the small black hole's photon ring. Finally, we also compare our results with recent numerical simulations by other groups, despite the dissimilar mass ratios considered.

</details>

Abstract: The influence of the low-frequency gravitational waves coupled with electromagnetic waves in material media on the test masses is investigated. The propagation of coupled gravitational waves in rarefied gases and cold magnetized plasma is considered. It has been shown that under specific conditions the amplitude of the coupled gravitational waves in a media reaches values of the order of the amplitude of transverse gravitational waves from external astrophysical sources. ### [27] [Dual Cutler-Vallisneri Corrections: Mitigating PSD Drift in Zero-Latency Gravitational-Wave Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09132)
*James Kennington*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对最小相位白化引起的频谱漂移问题的微扰框架，推导了定时、相位和信噪比偏差的解析表达式，并验证其误差小于1%；应用于GWTC-4.0数据表明，未校正的漂移会导致严重系统误差，而解析校正对维持探测体积与定位精度至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最小相位白化虽可实现零延迟，但会因实时功率谱密度（PSD）漂移导致匹配滤波度量失真，进而影响引力波探测的定时、相位和信噪比精度。

Method: 发展基于Cutler-Vallisneri形式的广义微扰框架，推导频谱漂移引起的定时、相位及SNR偏差解析公式，并通过稳态相位模型和数值注入验证。

Result: 校正后偏差误差<1%；在GWTC-4.0事件中，未校正漂移导致探测器对定时偏差超200μs、相位偏移达0.2 rad、天空定位误差5°–10°、SNR中值损失3–5%（极端达8%）。

Conclusion: 最小相位白化虽提升预警时间，但必须结合所提出的解析漂移校正，才能保障未来观测运行中的探测灵敏度与天区定位精度。

Abstract: Maximizing pre-merger warning times in gravitational-wave searches requires minimizing algorithmic latency. While current pipelines typically rely on truncated linear-phase filters, minimum-phase whitening offers a zero-latency alternative that eliminates the acausal look-ahead buffer. However, this causal approach exposes the analysis to spectral drift, where the whitening operator applied to live data diverges from the static template bank, creating a functional perturbation of the matched-filter metric. We develop a perturbative framework generalizing the Cutler-Vallisneri formalism to address these metric errors, deriving analytic expressions for the resulting timing, phase, and SNR biases. Validated against exact stationary-phase models and numerical injections, these corrections achieve $<1\%$ error. Applying this framework to GWTC-4.0 events with realistic 1-week power spectral density (PSD) lags, we find that uncorrected drift induces severe systematics: detector-pair timing biases exceeding $200 μ$s, phase shifts up to 0.2 rad, and sky-localization errors of $5^{\circ}-10^{\circ}$. Additionally, we observe a median signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) loss of $3-5\%$, with outliers exceeding $8\%$. These results demonstrate that while minimum-phase whitening maximizes the early-warning window, analytic drift corrections are essential to maintain detection volume and pointing accuracy in future observing runs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 改进基于有效啁啾质量的phenomenological模型，引入新像素采集法与时频域多阶偏心谐波能量乘积构建似然函数，并融合各谐波间能量比信息进行贝叶斯式采样估计。

Abstract: The events detected by the LIGO Virgo KAGRA collaboration over a period of 10 years have yielded a treasure trove of signals from compact binary coalescences. None of these events have shown a confident signature of eccentricity. With upgrades to the existing network and potential next generation gravitational wave detectors, we will be able to see much further into the universe increasing the likelihood of detecting eccentric systems. We improve upon the phenomenological approach of providing eccentricity constraints using an effective chirp mass model in the time frequency domain. We introduce an improved pixel collection method along with a likelihood based sampling approach inspired by Bayesian parameter estimation. Our approach constructs a likelihood from the product of energies collected across different eccentric harmonics in the time frequency representation. This formulation enables coarse but meaningful constraints on orbital eccentricity. Additionally, we incorporate information from the energy ratios between eccentric harmonics, further refining the eccentricity estimates. We test our approach on 500 non spinning equal mass eccentric systems and demonstrate that we can constrain the eccentricity within 0.2 around the true value. Moreover, our approach can deliver these constraints in 5 minutes on a machine with 50 cores. These results demonstrate that our phenomenological approach provides fast and reasonably accurate eccentricity estimates, making it a promising tool for rapid gravitational wave data analysis.

Abstract: Gravitational wave searches rely on a combination of methods, including matched filtering, coherent analyses, and more recent machine learning based pipelines. We investigate a hybrid approach that combines matched-filtering concepts with Convolutional Neural Networks, enabling efficient signal searches without relying on the usual $χ^2$ rejection test. Using simulated data sets that include injected signals in Gaussian noise, transient noise, and physical effects not represented in template bank, such as eccentricity, precession and higher-order modes, we show that the method achieves a detection efficiency comparable to a standard matched-filtering search while offering a more resource efficient pipeline.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The use of physical phenomena in the strong-field regime has become a primarily methodology for probing quantum-corrected gravity. This paper investigates periodic orbits, gravitational waves, and accretion disk radiation for a quantum-corrected black hole without Cauchy horizons. First, by analyzing the trajectory equations of massive particles in the equatorial plane, we study the influence of the quantum parameter $ζ$ on the stability of circular orbits. The results show that an increase in $ζ$ leads to an outward migration of both the innermost stable circular orbit and the marginally bound orbit, accompanied by an increase in the required specific angular momentum for particle motion on these two orbits. Then, we further investigate the periodic orbit characteristics of particles and compute the associated gravitational waveforms for extreme mass-ratio inspirals. It is demonstrated that quantum corrections induce a cumulative phase shift in the gravitational wave signal, leading to significant dephasing compared to the classical Schwarzschild case. Furthermore, based on the Novikov-Thorne thin accretion disk model, we evaluate the radiation characteristics of the accretion disk around this quantum-corrected black hole. The results indicate that the introduction of the quantum parameter suppresses the radiant energy flux, effective temperature, and overall radiative efficiency of the disk. These distinctive dynamical and radiative deviations provide potential phenomenological support for distinguishing quantum-corrected geometries from classical black holes using multiple observational means in the future.

### [32] [Shadows of quintessence black holes: spherical accretion, photon trajectories, and geodesic observers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09159)
*Ji-Wen Li,Zi-Liang Wang,Tao-Tao Sui*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准黑洞阴影分析通常假设观测者静止于空间无穷远，但在类精质修正的非渐近平直时空下，这种假设不适用，因此需考虑自由下落（测地线）观测者。

Method: 采用微扰方法推导事件视界位置、光子球半径、最内稳定圆轨道及临界撞击参数的解析表达式，并计算静态与自由下落球对称吸积流下的观测强度分布。

Result: 发现光子球半径和临界撞击参数是时空固有属性，但阴影的表观角尺寸强烈依赖于观测者的运动状态和位置；自由下落观测者测得的角半径更小，而自由上行者更大；在M87*的EHT观测中，更负的状态方程给出更强的类精质参数约束。

Conclusion: 在非渐近平直黑洞时空的阴影研究中，观测者的选取至关重要，不能仅依赖撞击参数刻画角结构，必须明确指定观测者模型。

Abstract: The presence of a quintessence-like field can influence the black hole shadow through three primary mechanisms: the dynamics of accretion flows, the trajectories of photons, and the motion of observers. Unlike standard shadow analyses that assume a static observer at spatial infinity, the non-asymptotically flat nature of quintessence-corrected spacetimes motivates the consideration of freely falling (geodesic) observers. Using a perturbative approach, we derive analytical expressions for the event-horizon location, photon-sphere radius, innermost stable circular orbit, and critical impact parameter. We compute the observed intensity profiles for both static and infalling spherical accretion flows. We find that, although the photon-sphere radius and the critical impact parameter are invariant properties of the spacetime, the apparent angular size of the shadow depends sensitively on the observer's motion and location. Freely infalling observers systematically measure smaller angular radii than static observers at the same radius, whereas freely outgoing observers measure larger ones, in agreement with relativistic aberration. In contrast to the Schwarzschild case, the impact parameter alone is insufficient to characterize the observed angular structure in non-asymptotically flat spacetimes. Applying our results to the Event Horizon Telescope observation of M87$^\ast$, we show that more negative equations of state lead to stronger constraints on the quintessence parameter, largely independent of the observer prescription. Our analysis highlights the importance of carefully specifying the observer in shadow studies of non-asymptotically flat black-hole spacetimes.

We construct three distinct geometries exhibiting this behavior using different representations of constant-curvature spaces. Method: 结合渐近迭代法（AIM）、WKB近似法和Bernstein谱方法计算准正规模频率（QNFs），其中Bernstein方法专用于l=0标量扰动以提供高精度验证；灰体因子（GFs）采用WKB方法计算。

Result: 1) AIM与WKB结果高度一致；2) Bernstein谱法确认l=0标量扰动QNFs的可靠性；3) 磁荷Qm与EH耦合参数ε显著影响QNFs的实部（振荡频率）与虚部（衰减率）以及灰体因子的穿透率；4) Λ与l也调控QNM行为。

Conclusion: 磁荷与非线性EH效应共同调制dS黑洞的扰动谱与散射特性，表明其在强场引力检验与早期宇宙模型中具有潜在重要性；多种数值方法的协同验证提升了结果可信度。

Abstract: This paper investigates the perturbation dynamics of massless scalar and electromagnetic fields on magnetically charged de Sitter (dS) black holes within the framework of string-inspired Euler-Heisenberg (EH) gravity. We calculate the quasinormal frequencies (QNFs) and discuss the influences of black hole magnetic charge $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$, the cosmological constant $Λ$, coupling parameter $ε$ and multipole number $l$ on QNFs, emphasizing the relationships between these parameters and quasinormal modes (QNMs) behavior. We find that the results obtained through the asymptotic iteration method (AIM) are in good agreement with those obtained by the WKB method. Importantly, the Bernstein spectral method is employed as a rigorous cross-check for QNFs in the $l=0$ scalar perturbation sector, where the WKB approximation is often unreliable. The greybody factor (GFs) is calculated using WKB method. The effects of the parameters $Q_{\mathrm{m}}$ and $ε$ on the greybody factor are also studied.

</details>


### [35] [Relativistic Corrections to the Formation Rate of Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09547)
*Chen Feng,Yong Tang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个相对论自洽的解析框架来估计极端质量比旋进（EMRI）事件率，通过引入能量依赖的角动量损失锥和广义相对论导出的最小稳定半径，显著提升了预测速率（约8倍），凸显了相对论效应对空间引力波探测器（如LISA、太极）的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EMRI是空间引力波探测器（如LISA、太极）的关键目标，但其形成率预测严重依赖于对相对论效应（如损失锥定义、稳定轨道半径）的准确建模；传统牛顿方法可能严重低估真实率。

Method: 在Schwarzschild时空中，将经典损失锥角动量推广为能量依赖量，并用广义相对论给出的最小稳定轨道半径修正 plunging 近心点；结合角动量扩散与引力波耗散的动力学模型，构建相对论自洽的解析率估算框架。

Result: 相比牛顿处理，引入相对论效应使EMRI预测率提高约8倍；该增强效应对恒星密度轮廓越浅越显著，且与中心大质量黑洞质量无关。

Conclusion: 相对论效应（特别是损失锥和稳定轨道的相对论修正）对EMRI事件率预测至关重要，忽略它们将导致系统性低估，影响LISA等任务的科学预期与数据解读。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are long-duration gravitational-wave sources in which a compact object gradually spirals into a massive black hole. Their formation is governed by the interplay between stochastic angular-momentum diffusion driven by two-body relaxation and the dissipative evolution caused by gravitational-wave emission, with the loss-cone boundary deciding whether an object undergoes an inspiral or a direct plunge. Building on this physical picture, we construct a relativistically self-consistent analytic framework for estimating EMRI event rates. In Schwarzschild spacetime, we generalize the standard loss-cone angular momentum to an energy-dependent quantity and revise the plunge pericenter by using the minimum stable radius derived from general relativity. Relative to the Newtonian treatment, we show that incorporating these relativistic effects increases the predicted EMRI rates by roughly a factor of 8. This enhancement becomes more pronounced for shallower stellar density profiles and is insensitive to the mass of the central massive black hole, which emphasizes that relativistic effects are essential for EMRI rate estimations that are relevant for space-based gravitational-wave detectors, such as LISA and Taiji.

### [36] [Dynamics of quadratic f(R) cosmology with a perfect fluid: Jordan and Einstein frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09667)
*Artur Alho,Margarida Lima,Filipe C. Mena*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了纯二次引力理论在空间平坦、均匀各向同性宇宙模型中的全局动力学行为，通过构建约旦框架和爱因斯坦框架下的三维全局正则动力系统，结合单调性分析、不变边界轨道结构刻画及非双曲不动点的去奇异化，给出了完整的相流及其极限集描述，并借助渐近展开识别了两框架间全局共形映射的有效解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入约旦框架和共形相关的爱因斯坦框架下的全局正则三维动力系统；在约旦框架中利用内流单调性、二维不变边界轨道结构及非双曲不动点的去奇异化；在爱因斯坦框架中利用状态空间的斜积结构和不变边界轨道分析；并借助渐近展开判断解在两框架间的共形可映射性。

Result: 获得了两个框架下动力系统的完整全局相图与极限集分类；明确了哪些解可通过全局共形变换在两框架间对应，哪些不能；揭示了二次引力宇宙模型的典型长期演化行为。

Conclusion: 纯二次引力理论在空间平坦FLRW宇宙中具有丰富的全局动力学结构，其行为不仅依赖于物质内容，还显著受所选框架（约旦或爱因斯坦）影响；全局分析表明，框架选择直接影响解的存在性与物理可解释性。

Abstract: We investigate the global dynamics of the field equations of (pure) quadratic theories of gravity which generalise Einstein's theory in spatially flat homogeneous and isotropic cosmological models with a perfect fluid. We introduce global and regular 3-dimensional dynamical systems' formulations, on both the Jordan frame and the conformally related Einstein frame. The analysis in the Jordan frame explores the monotonicity properties of the interior flow which, together with the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries and the desingularisation of non-hyperbolic fixed points, provides a global description of the flow and its limit sets. In the Einstein frame, the analysis uses the skew-product structure of the Einstein state space and the characterisation of the orbit structure on the 2-dimensional invariant boundaries. Furthermore, by obtaining asymptotic expansions we identify the solutions that are global conformally mapped from the Jordan frame to the Einstein frame and those that are not.

*Gianni Boschetti,Miguel Campiglia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Compère-Gralla-Wei渐近框架下，仅利用爱因斯坦方程在类时、类空和类光无穷远附近的性质及区域间匹配条件，协变地推导出经典对数软引力子定理；揭示了标准对数软因子中未来与过去硬粒子不对称性的根源在于空间无穷远处引力场的已知不连续性，并纳入了入射软辐射的贡献。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于Compère-Gralla-Wei渐近框架，严格运用爱因斯坦方程在类时、类空和类光无穷远附近的结构，结合不同无穷远区域间的匹配条件进行协变推导。

Result: 给出了完全时间反演协变的对数软引力子定理推导；证明了标准对数软因子的不对称性源于空间无穷远处引力场的固有不连续性；并自然包含了入射软辐射的贡献。

Conclusion: 对数软定理本质上是广义相对论在多重无穷远区域协同约束下的必然结果，其看似不对称的形式实则反映了时空整体渐近结构（尤其是空间无穷远）的深层特性；该框架为统一处理进/出软辐射和记忆效应提供了协变基础。

Abstract: We present a derivation of the classical log soft graviton theorem within the asymptotic framework of Compère, Gralla, and Wei. The proof relies solely on Einstein equations near timelike, spatial, and null infinity, together with matching properties across these regions. The approach is fully covariant under time reversal and incorporates contributions from incoming soft radiation. In the absence of incoming memory one recovers the standard log soft factor, which features an asymmetry between future and past hard components. From an asymptotic perspective, the origin of this asymmetry lies in a long-known discontinuity of the gravitational field at spatial infinity.

### [38] [Globally stable, ghost-free hyperbolic square-root deformation of the Starobinsky model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09944)
*Andrei Galiautdinov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种精确解析的Starobinsky模型变形，通过构造一个严格正导数的f(R)函数（含双曲平方根形式），消除了二次f(R)引力中因f'(R)=0导致的强耦合奇点；该模型在低曲率下恢复广义相对论，在高正曲率下保持慢滚暴胀平台，并保证全局无鬼、无快子，支持非奇异反弹宇宙学，且预言的ns和r值符合Planck与BICEP/Keck观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 消除二次f(R)引力中因f'(R)=0导致的强耦合奇点，同时保留Starobinsky模型在暴胀和低能极限下的成功特性，并实现全局健康的理论行为（如无鬼、无快子、非奇异反弹）。

Method: 构造具有严格正导数的f(R)函数：f'(R) = αR + √(α²R² + 1)，推导其对应的f(R)形式；在Jordan与Einstein帧下分析标量场（scalaron）动力学、势能、稳定性及宇宙学解；计算CMB观测量ns与r。

Result: 确保f'(R) > 0全局成立，从而消除病态分支与强耦合奇点；标量子质量平方恒正，理论全局鬼/快子自由；Einstein帧中得到全局定义的势能V(φ)，形成φ→−∞时的不可穿越能量壁垒，支持稳定非奇异反弹；预测ns ≈ 0.967，r ≈ 0.00083，与当前观测高度一致。

Conclusion: 该超几何平方根f(R)模型是Starobinsky理论的一个健康、可检验的推广，兼具理论自洽性（无奇点、无病态自由度）与可观测性（符合CMB精密数据），为暴胀与早期宇宙反弹提供了新范式。

Abstract: We propose an exact, analytic deformation of the Starobinsky model governed by the strictly positive derivative of its Lagrangian, $f'(R) = αR + \sqrt{α^2 R^2 + 1}$, with $α> 0$. This geometric hyperbolic square-root ansatz is designed to eliminate the well-known strong-coupling singularity that arises in quadratic $f(R)$ gravity when $f'(R)=0$. The construction seamlessly recovers general relativity at low curvatures and preserves the successful slow-roll inflationary plateau at extreme positive curvatures. In the limit $R \to -\infty$, the derivative $f'(R)$ asymptotes to zero strictly from above, removing the pathological branch associated with the vanishing of $f'(R)$. This guarantees that the only admissible constant-curvature ($R=A$) solutions correspond to standard Einstein spaces with an effective cosmological constant $Λ_{\text{eff}} \equiv A/4$. The first and second derivatives of the action, as well as the scalaron mass squared, remain strictly positive globally, ensuring a perfectly ghost-free and tachyon-free cosmological evolution across the entire spacetime manifold. In the Einstein frame, the dynamics of the scalaron is governed by the globally defined potential $V(φ) = \frac{1}{8α} [ 1 - (1 + 2\sqrt{2/3}φ) \exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ) ] + Λ\exp(-2\sqrt{2/3}φ)$, which naturally establishes an impenetrable energetic wall as $φ\to -\infty$, offering a robust, globally stable mechanism for non-singular bouncing cosmologies. For $N = 60$ inflationary e-folds, the model predicts a scalar spectral index of $n_s \simeq 0.967$ and a strongly suppressed tensor-to-scalar ratio of $r \simeq 0.00083$, which position the proposed theory within the observationally favored parameter space of the Planck and BICEP/Keck Array baseline constraints.

</details>


### [39] [Strong deflection of massive particles via the geodesic deviation equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09946)
*Takahisa Igata,Yohsuke Takamori*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了静态球对称时空下类时测地线粒子散射的强偏转极限新公式，揭示了偏转角对数发散系数与不稳定圆轨道径向不稳定性指数之间的协变关系，并将其用轨道处局部曲率数据表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强引力场中粒子运动的普适行为，特别是接近不稳定圆轨道时的散射特性及其几何和物理根源。

Method: 基于类时测地线运动，利用测地线偏差方程协变推导强偏转极限下偏转角的对数发散形式，并将发散系数与径向不稳定性指数关联，再通过局部曲率张量将其显式表达。

Result: 证明了对数发散系数等于以方位角为单位的径向不稳定性指数；该指数可完全由不稳定圆轨道上的局部曲率数据决定；在广义相对论中，其物质依赖性仅通过一个由静止系能量密度与径向、切向压强构成的标量组合体现。

Conclusion: 强偏转极限具有清晰的几何（曲率）与动力学（不稳定性）双重诠释，为黑洞阴影、引力透镜等现象提供了更本质的理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a formulation of the strong deflection limit for the scattering of particles following timelike geodesics in asymptotically flat, static, and spherically symmetric spacetimes. For fixed specific energy, as the angular momentum approaches its critical value from above, the particle passes arbitrarily close to the associated unstable circular orbit, undergoes many windings around it, and the deflection angle diverges logarithmically. Using the geodesic deviation equation, we show covariantly that the coefficient of this logarithmic divergence is determined by the radial instability exponent of the critical trajectory, defined per unit azimuthal angle. We express this instability exponent in terms of local curvature data on the unstable circular orbit, thereby providing both kinematic and geometric interpretations of the strong deflection limit. In general relativity, its matter dependence enters only through a single local scalar combination constructed from the static-frame energy density and the principal radial and tangential pressures.

### [40] [Interaction of the gravitational Hawking radiation and a static point mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.09948)
*João P. B. Brito,Atsushi Higuchi,Luís C. B. Crispino*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了静态点质量（由弦支撑）在史瓦西黑洞外部与霍金辐射引力子的相互作用，推导出其在Unruh态下对热引力子总响应率的闭式解析表达式，并指出黑洞尺寸起自然红外截断作用；该响应率在Hartle-Hawking态下为零，故两态下总响应率相同，此现象在电磁场中也成立，但在无质量标量场中不成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解黑洞背景下量子场与经典源（如静态点质量）的相互作用，特别是红外发散行为如何被黑洞几何所调控。

Method: 基于Unruh态和Hartle-Hawking态，计算静态点质量-弦系统对热引力子的响应率，对比Rindler时空中的红外发散行为，分析黑洞视界附近的有效红外截断机制。

Result: 获得响应率的闭式解析解；证实黑洞尺寸提供自然红外截断，使响应率有限；发现Hartle-Hawking态中入射引力子贡献为零，故两量子态下总响应率相同；该结论适用于引力子和光子，但不适用于无质量标量子。

Conclusion: 黑洞时空几何可消除加速系中常见的红外发散，Unruh态与Hartle-Hawking态对静态源的净量子效应等价，揭示了黑洞量子真空结构的独特性及其与平直时空的深刻差异。

Abstract: We study the interaction of a stress-energy tensor describing a static point mass supported by a string outside a Schwarzschild black hole with the gravitons of the Hawking radiation. We derive a closed-form analytic expression for the total response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons in the Unruh state, which models the quantum state in the spacetime of a spherically symmetric black hole formed by gravitational collapse. This response rate is finite in contrast with the infrared divergent response rate for a static point mass supported by a string in Rindler spacetime, i.e., a point mass accelerated uniformly by a string in Minkowski spacetime. By comparing the response rate near the black hole horizon with that in Rindler spacetime, we show that the size of the black hole acts as a natural infrared cutoff. We also find that the response rate of this stress-energy tensor to the thermal gravitons incoming from past null infinity in the Hartle-Hawking state vanishes. As a result, the total response rate of a static point mass (supported by a string) in the Unruh and Hartle-Hawking states for gravitons are identical. This is also the case for a static charge interacting with the electromagnetic field but not for a static source for a massless scalar field.
